        <div style="text-align: center; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Trump Media and Partners Announce Launch of Separately Managed Accounts</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic;">New Partnership Debuts America-First Themed Investment Vehicles</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: justify; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SARASOTA, Fla., January 13, 2026 (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) --<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">&#160;</font>Trump Media and Technology Group Corp.
          (Nasdaq, NYSE Texas: DJT) (&#8220;Trump Media&#8221; or &#8220;the Company&#8221;), operator of the social media platform Truth Social, the streaming platform Truth+, and the fintech brand Truth.Fi, along with Yorkville America Equities LLC (&#8220;Yorkville America
          Equities&#8221;), an America-First asset management firm, and Index <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Technologies Group, LLC (&#8220;ITG&#8221;), an originator </font>and provider of thematic investment solutions, today <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">announced the launch of four new Truth Social&#8211;branded Separately Managed Account (&#8220;SMA&#8221;) i</font>nvestment strategies developed by ITG and based on American values and priorities.</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Trump Media has provided the seed investment to launch these strategies, which give investors access to portfolios built around American values
          and priorities. The initial lineup includes:</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="zb625431e68b74a689a67873719b63fbe" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

            <tr>
              <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
              </td>
              <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8226;</td>
              <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: justify;">
                <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">Truth Social Made in America: </font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">a high-conviction,
                    rules-based strategy that leverages proprietary data and algorithms to invest in U.S. companies we believe are driving industrial growth, domestic production, workforce expansion, and technological innovation, strengthening national
                    resilience and advancing America&#8217;s economic renewal.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>

        </table>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z5a573ad400134800898f436ebf32b3f0" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

            <tr>
              <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
              </td>
              <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8226;</td>
              <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: justify;">
                <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">Truth Social Liberty &amp; Security: </font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">a patriotic strategy
                    that allocates capital to U.S. and allied companies advancing national security and the Department of War&#8217;s 14 critical and emerging technologies, such as advanced computing, software, cyber security, space technology, energy storage,
                    artificial intelligence, and microelectronics, while safeguarding global trade and avoiding firms that support what are felt to be adversarial interests. </font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>

        </table>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="ze0c401cb1bd94e60861c125b0a57569c" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

            <tr>
              <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
              </td>
              <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8226;</td>
              <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: justify;">
                <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">Truth Social Christian Values</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">: progressing beyond
                    prohibited industry groups and allocating to companies that we think have cultures, policies, and practices that demonstrate integrity and align with the framework for economic life, biblically responsible principals and Christian
                    values generally.&#160; </font></div>
              </td>

              <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: justify;">
                <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">Truth Social Energy and Essential Services</font><font style="font-size: 10pt;">: strives to
                    provide efficient exposure to essential infrastructure and services, spanning energy, utilities, water, data centers, satellites, semiconductors, and telecommunications, by focusing on operators that we believe underpin long-term
                    economic growth and consistent demand.</font></div>

        <div style="text-align: justify; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal;">&#8220;The launch of these strategies represents a milestone in the expansion of our financial services effort,&#8221; said Devin Nunes, CEO and Chairman of
          Trump Media. &#8220;We are proud to seed this initiative with Trump Media&#8217;s own capital and to introduce investment products that not only support innovative companies across critical sectors of the U.S. economy but also remain firmly aligned with our
          core values.&#8221;</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: justify; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8220;Yorkville America Equities, Trump Media, and ITG bring together complementary expertise in asset management, media, and technology to deliver what we believe is a
          unique offering for today&#8217;s investors,&#8221; said Troy Rillo, CEO of Yorkville America Equities. &#8220;These strategies are designed to align capital with American innovation and values to provide investors with patriotic thematic portfolios.&#8221; </div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: justify; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8220;At ITG, we believe that investing is about more than returns, it&#8217;s about values,&#8221; said Jon DuPrau, Managing Partner at ITG. &#8220;These SMAs are built on proprietary,
          data-driven frameworks that combine financial performance with values-based scoring, empowering investors to combine prudent investing principles with their convictions, while participating in what we believe is one of the most important economic
          transformations of our time.&#8221;</div>
        <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
        <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Each SMA strategy is systematically constructed using ITG&#8217;s proprietary algorithms and is rebalanced quarterly to reflect market dynamics while
          maintaining alignment with thematic objectives.&#160; </div>

          content; and Truth.Fi, a financial services and FinTech brand incorporating America First investment vehicles.</div>
